< review>
What a GREAT beach access in Carmel by the Sea!! Cool temps, saw a teenager have a surprise birthday party, easy access with stone steps, a spicket to rinse your feet off with, and plenty of space to put your blanket. The water was ice cold but there was somebody there with the professional camera and zoom lens in the water taking pictures of two Surfers. The view is absolutely gorgeous and the smoke from all the fires was not bad. Then we went to eat at Portobello and it was wonderful! La great place to visit</review>

<review>Fantastic spot that many people don't know about when visiting Pebble Beach. You have to time the tides or access will be under water. If you know where to go, you can cut through the golf course and the a set of stairs down. Plenty of errant golf balls to pick up and the views are incredible on a sunny day. I'm not sure if you can access the beach without a resident badge or if you can pay to get in, but it's worth it.</review><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNTErwb71FIY0FGfx5DlHdPz9fWpyIrSPJjdvA_=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics><Response>None<//Response></record></dataset><record>

< Text>
We came here on a Monday night around 7:00, there was plenty of empty tables, though not much street parking.  They have standard Korean menu with Bim Bim Bop (hot stone rice bowl) and tofu soup.  On this rainy night, we were not offered hot tea of any type, only room temperature water.  The service isn't great here, we only saw the waitress 4 times on a very quiet night.  The food was ok, I found other places to have a larger assortment of Ban Chan (side dishes) offered, especially at dinner time.  The Bim Bim Bop was good because they heated the stone bowl enough to form a good crust on the rice.  They have Korean BBQ grill, but at the price they're charging, I would go to an all you can eat place in Korean town which would be able to same price as one order of meat here.<//Text>

<Review>Not only is the name of the place clever (and hilarious), the food is delicious, authentic, and well-priced. The ambiance is of a classic Korean bar, so if you are looking for a quieter evening, plan to visit on a weekday or earlier in the evening. The wait staff is phenomenal, extremely patient and attentive.
Menu wise, you have many classic boon-shik (분식) items like pork bone soup, bibimbap, bulgogi, and etc. but also have some classics that I would have not expected on American soil. Great drinking place, with both flavoured soju and soju cocktails, as well as other options.
I highly recommend this place. It's right off of the MUNI line!<//Review>< Pictures>

<Name>Alan Lin</Name><user_id>101526974547596800160</user_id>< Resp>
None</Resp>
< rating>
3< /rating>
<Time>1471204587380<//Time>< review>
Came here after getting a recommendation from a friend. Got here around 9pm and was seated immediately. The seating was comfortable, there are booths and tables are spaced out enough to provide privacy and allow you to talk with your mates at the table without yelling at each other.

Food: The presentation of the food was good, large white places with food centered for contrast. The taste of the food were a little on the mild side in terms of spiciness (hot). Depending on your crave, this place might suit your taste. If you have friends who are less tolerable to spice food, this is the place to bring them.

Service: The servers were really nice and accommodating. The table that was open when we came in was situated by the door and was tad chilly. We said we preferred another seating if possible and we were approached by the server 2 minutes later when a table left, telling us that she will clean the table right away and transition us over if we would like. They servers to get fairly busy and gives out the sense that the place is short staffed when the late evening crowd comes in, HOWEVER, if you just quickly tell the what you need as they run by, they WILL get to the matter.

Overall: I enjoyed the place for what it is and I will revisit, but I don't think I will be selective to whom I will bring depending on the taste buds of my friend, whether they like that heavier spiciness that are present in a lot of other Korean restaurants or whether they are into the lighter end of the Scoville scale. I would suggest going before 10 because the place was packed shortly after my food arrived and there was a queue when I was leaving the place.

Ordered:
Kimchi Fried Rice with beef- Everyone enjoyed it, very flavorful
Tofu Soup - It was decent, I enjoyed it. Some people thinks it could use a tad more flavor
Grilled Squid with butter - very aromatic; lots of ginger, garlic, and onion
Korean Fried Chicken Wings - Didn't really stand out, but wasn't bad. The wings weren't dry.
Soju Cocktails - I enjoyed them, they weren't overly sweet and you can still catch the hint of soju

What I forgot to tried and was strongly recommended by my friend was the corn with mozzarella cheese.<//review>

<Text>I recently tried the  wings  at the Fire Wings located at the Haven City  Market, and after some reflection, I have to say the food was pretty good. I tried their traditional buffalo wings, their dragon wings, and seasoned fries. All were good, though the dragon wings were exceptional. From  what I could find on the web Fire Wings started off in Northern California and is quickly growing.  They offer many different seasons and dry rub with an asian twist. Overall, I have no major complaints. The staff was friendly. The food was good, and the prices were decent. They also offer beers on draft and in cans. My only concern, though,  was  the temperature of my food. It was cold. Whenever I get cold food, I'm lead to believe my food was precooked and sitting around for awhile. You always hear experts say: cold food should be kept cold and hot food,  hot.  Either way this place is cool, check it out.< /Text>< pics>

<rating>3</rating><Text>Visited Fire Wings Rancho Cucamonga on Easter Sunday with the family; we usually go to the Brea location and we love it, but since we were in the Rancho Cucamonga area, we decided to check this place out. We might have gone on a bad day because the customer service was horrible.

When we got there, nobody was at the front counter to assist us (waited approximately 10 mins for someone to assist us). We ordered the 40 piece family pack (40 wings in 4 different flavors, large fries, large side and veggies) and the worker did not even ask what we wanted for our large size. We just got two orders of fries with our order.

When we went to the counter again to ask for a cup of water, some of the workers were gathered deciding whose turn it was to go on break, while another girl was trying her best to not make eye contact with us.

The wings were delicious (which is why I'm rating this place a 3 stars, despite the bad customer service). We recommend the salt and pepper wing flavor (dry rub) and the korean flavor (very saucy).<//Text>< pictures>

The reason I have to give them a 2 star is because if the customer service. I’ve come to this location every Tuesday and Thursday for the past month. <user_name>Dan Mullin<//user_name><date>1443450048097< /date><Rate>4</Rate><Review>My wife and I kind of expected to get the typical "tourist treatment" this close to the beach but The Terrace Cafe was nothing like that! Service was good, especially for a Friday night, and food was plentiful. Prices were reasonable. Pints of decent beer were $6 each. We split a dozen shrimp tempura (very large shrimp), a huge bacon-avocado cheese burger, fries, and two brews and were out the door for $40 plus tip. Not cheap but very reasonable and the sea breeze is worth something. The owner made it a point to circulate to make sure all was well with his customers. It was good to see.</Review><pics>None</pics><Resp>None</Resp>< gmapID>

< Review>
This is a wall of text, but Sara Brown at DeWitt saved my life.
I injured my back and could not move and thought my life might be over and I could never do anything fun again. When I started with Sara I could bailey stand, walk, sleep or just breath. At first, she just worked with me to find a position that would make it feel better just while I held the position. I had not been able to find anything like that myself. Then she helped me find positions and exercised that helped me feel better for a few minutes afterwards. Every week my exercised were adjusted to what I could do and changes slightly. Eventually I was just doing four exercises and I would do them every morning when I woke up, every night before bed, and every morning when I woke up again at about 3 am. from the pain. Sometimes the exercised made me feel well enough to even go back to sleep. When I got to that point the progression was noticeably faster and I was only seeing Sara every other week. My core is stronger than it has ever been in my life and I’ve recently graduated from PT and have just finished the fundamentals CrossFit class so I can stay strong and not injure myself again. It was a long process and especially in the beginning I felt helpless and hopeless. Now I feel like I can change my lifetime of habits and be strong and agile despite my age and desk job. Sara really paid attention and there were a few times when it was not easy to figure out what was going on, but she figured it out and guided me to a much better place. Thank you Sara!< /Review>

<time>1555462100563<//time><Rate>3< /Rate>< Review>
Today we rented a large storage unit from Emmanuel at Public Storage. The unit seems OK, although it has 2 large water stains on the wood floor near the door so I don't know if we will have water intrusion or mold problems there. Emmanuel was polite and knowledgeable, but you should be ready for MAJOR UPSELLS when you go in there!! He said we have to buy their type of lock so we did even though we brought 2 of our own with us, and we could not rent the unit without immediate insurance coverage -  purchased directly from them for a minimum of $11/month. All they had to do was tell us that before we showed up for our appointment so that we would have known ALL the costs in advance, rather than springing it on us at the time we rented the unit. Since nothing was mentioned about that in advance, we showed up with a moving truck with our things and were surprised to be required to buy a different lock and overpriced insurance on the spot, feeling a bit ripped off. But we have already notified AAA and learned that storage unit coverage is of course already provided through our renter's insurance policy for NO ADDITIONAL CHARGE and have added it so we can cancel the Public Storage insurance next month. So be aware. He also tried to sell us boxes, which we declined, and some sort of anti-humidifying crystals to keep moisture out of the unit - which we bought (a gimmick? I don't know - definitely didn't keep the moisture off of the floor in there!). So, overall, the facility seems OK and Emmanuel is polite, but we didn't appreciate being forced to buy another lock and insurance on the spot when we weren't told in advance these exact things would be required at the time of renting so that we could have arranged for them in advance. Despite the fact we spent more money than what cost was represented to us in advance, we are hoping things will go well and our belongings will be protected while we're there!!<//Review>

< review>
If anyone needs storage for a couple months this is the place to be! They made moving so easy, and helped you with any questions you may have. I don't like the business aspect, but the service was amazing! 5 stars for the service Sadik & Masoma . They were nice honest people and found me the best price possible. However there were some flaws about this place for instances the pricing were a bit high but lucky i got a storage unit during the memorial day special so i only had to pay $60 a month for a 5x10 unit. Which was a killer deal. But beware of the hidden fees the company charges, $22 for an admin expense for setting everything up, $22 for a lock ( you must buy their locks), and also don't buy the moving boxes and packing supplies here, they are way too overpriced. At home depot you can get the same box for a quarter of the price. For a company that specializes in moving and storage units, you got to have way cheaper prices than the competition. (in my opinion) Also you may want to wash down the street, parts of the street when i was walking had a foul smell. Also the neighboring units next to each other looked like it was divided by a thin piece of drywall so it looks easy to break into not sure if it was with all the units but i wouldn't feel safe holding anything to valuables in there. I wish there was a trash bin near by incase you have something you no longer wanted. other than that I would have given the business 2.5 stars but the service is what got the 5 stars.

- Kevin< /review>

< Text>
WARNING: DO NOT DO BUSINESS WITH PUBLIC STORAGE. CLASS ACTION LAW SUIT FILED AGAINST CORPORATION DUE TO UNFAIR BUSINESS PRACTICES... PLENTY OF STORAGE PLACES IN THE SURROUNDING AREA NOW THEN EVER BEFORE.

The surrounding storage facilities offer much nicer grounds and access times, nevertheless price.

I'm a contractor using this location for my contracts. Morning access is absolutely with late access needed....

Storage facility and management is fine. Any write up on management is truth. Public Storage and the way they handle you is another story all by it self.

About 6 months ago, they had a building security breach. One of the buildings 2nd floor supposedly had been hit. Unit had bee broken into.  In this event, corporate decided without notice, to have access times to the property restricted. This can be controlled and given access for individuals or it can be locked down in a group setting. Just like if you are late on the bill, they can lock just you down. Management can override, if they choose. At least that is what was in the past.

However,  NO EMAIL, NO LETTERS, NO PHONE CALLS, NO GATE NOTICE.... NOTHING.... Official gate notice didn't show until weeks later.  Just a piece of paper with magic marker with new times.

No such effort whatsoever, was ever offered by this enterprise. Again the facility and management is fine. Building is extremely old but since the security breach, they installed a whole new security system, which of course is tied into your account. This can be controlled by Corp too. Management at this time can not override anything. Which in this case quenches the relationship with property management and the tenant.

Soon after the breach, my rent went up by $25 with no notice or any explanation. I wonder what this presents... tenants paying for the new upgrade of security.

When I first came to this property access was, 7am to 9pm. 14 hour access. After the breach, 9:30am to 5pm, half the time was cut off. So why am I paying for extra $25. They should be reducing my cost since now I lost half my access. Why isn't my storage half the cost now?

A class action suit will probably want us to be compensated for our losses, once they review the original contract... we'll see...

Public Storage has been horrible in doing business when managing with tenants. Upper management has not returned any calls, district/regional manager being rude and passing the buck instead of taking ownership.

Nothing has been done for any of the contractors who are using this facility after talking with a few. We all pick this place base on the same reason. Now we can't get to our supplies and tools to work a job with a fair and reasonable time frame. This Corp. controlled storage facility has cost me several contracts due to not being able to get to tools of the trade. I have only been able to get to it on weekends. Even those hours have been reduced. This has been the case now for over 6 months. The only thing that has been done at this time, they adjusted the access hour later to 6pm instead of 5pm. Still can't get to it in that time frame... Need the late access to return equipment and supplies nevertheless for the next work day.
RENT AT YOUR OWN RISK.< /Text>
